   google_tag_params = {
					edu_pid: "",
					edu_plocid: "Australia",

				};
			

			
				
				
				
				
				
				
				
				google_tag_params['function'] = location.pathname.startsWith('/lp/') ? 'landing' : 'general';
				google_tag_params['type'] = 'home';

				google_tag_params['sessionID'] = 'be717d1d-f65d-43ff-a5a7-4a15fe268c52';
				var width = $(window).width();
				if (width <= 720) var device = 'M';
				else if (width <= 980) var device = 'T';
				else var device = 'D';
				google_tag_params['Device'] = device;

				/* opti  stuff starts here */
				/* Read Create Delete Cookie functions */
				function createCookie(name,value,days) {
					if (days) {
						var date = new Date();
						date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
						var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
					}
					else var expires = "";
					document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
				}

				function readCookie(name) {
					var nameEQ = name + "=";
					var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
					for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
						var c = ca[i];
						while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
						if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
					}
					return null;
				}

				function eraseCookie(name) {
					createCookie(name,"",-1);
				}
				function getParameterByName(name, url) {
					if (!url) {
					  url = window.location.href;
					}
					name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, "\\$&");
					var regex = new RegExp("[?&]" + name + "(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)"),
						results = regex.exec(url);
					if (!results) return null;
					if (!results[2]) return '';
					return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, " "));
				}
				function CRUDCookie(cookieName, cookieValue){
					if(readCookie(cookieName)){
						//console.log('cookie exists');
						//console.log(cookieName);
						var cookieTemp = '';
						if(!cookieName.match(cookieValue)){
							//console.log('updating cookie');
							cookieTemp = readCookie(cookieName);
                            if (cookieTemp.indexOf(cookieValue) == -1){
							    eraseCookie(cookieName);
							    createCookie(cookieName,cookieTemp+ ", " +cookieValue,30);
                            }
						}else {
							//console.log(cookieValue+ ' already exists cookie');
						}
					}else{
						//console.log('creating new cookie ' +cookieName);
						createCookie(cookieName,cookieValue,30);
					}
				}
				/* end  */

				/* OPTI and DL  vars */

				/* course code */
				var OPTI = 'cecode';
				if(location.search.match('enquiry_sent')){
					var courseCode = getParameterByName('code');
				} else {
					var courseCode = '';
				}

				/* Area Code */
				var OPTIAreaCode = 'ceAreaCode';
				
					var leadAreaCode = '';
				

				if(getParameterByName('code') && location.search.match('enquiry_sent')){
					CRUDCookie(OPTI, courseCode);
					CRUDCookie(OPTIAreaCode, leadAreaCode);

					google_tag_params[OPTI] = readCookie(OPTI);
					google_tag_params[OPTIAreaCode] = readCookie(OPTIAreaCode);
				}

				/* end OPTI stuff */

									page_name:"Open Colleges | Online Courses Australia",
									url:"/",
								});
							} else {
								console.log('tiq undefined');
							};
						};
					};

    // This function is called by isMenuCategoriesClicked() function on the megamenu/desktop.js file
    function handleCourseCategoryClick(e) {
        var target_course_category = e.target.textContent.trim();
        var impressions = [];

        if (datalayer_course_categories[target_course_category] !== undefined) {
            var relevant_courses = datalayer_course_categories[target_course_category];
            for (var i = 0; i < relevant_courses.length; i++) {
                var course_dict = relevant_courses[i];
                var course = convertDictToArray(course_dict)[0];
                impressions.push({
                    'id': course.code,
                    'name': course.name,
                    'category': course.category,
                    'position': course.position,
                    'brand': course.brand,
                    'price': course.price,
                    'list': course.list
                });
            }
            pushCourseCategoryInfoToDataLayer(impressions);
        }
        handleCourseItemClick();
    }

    function pushCourseCategoryInfoToDataLayer(impressions) {
        dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'productImpression',
            'ecommerce': {
                'currencyCode': 'AUD', 
                'impressions':  impressions,
            }
        });
    }

    var courses = []
    var courses_dict = {}
    // Merging courses into one array
    convertDictToArray(datalayer_course_categories).forEach(function (category_courses) {
        courses = courses.concat(category_courses);
    });

    // Now merging all the data into a courses dictionary
    courses.forEach(function (course) {
        courses_dict = Object.assign({}, courses_dict, course);
    });

    function handleCourseItemClick() {
        var course_items = document.querySelectorAll("div.course-item li a");

        course_items.forEach(function (course_item) {
            course_item.onclick = function (e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
                var target_course_item_name = e.target.innerHTML;
                var products = [];

                var course = courses_dict[target_course_item_name];

                products.push({
                    'id': course.code,
                    'name': course.name,
                    'category': course.category,
                    'position': course.position,
                    'brand': course.brand,
                    'price': course.price,
                    'list': course.list
                });

                pushCourseItemInfoToDataLayer(course.list, products);


            }
        });
    }

    function pushCourseItemInfoToDataLayer(list,products) {
        dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'productClick',
            'ecommerce': {
                'click': {
                    'actionField': {'list': list},
                    'products': products,
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function convertDictToArray(dict) {
        return Object.keys(dict).map(function (e) {
            return dict[e];
        });
    }
  </script>

  function isCourseCategoryClicked() {
    var course_categories = document.querySelectorAll(".second-submenu a.icon");

    course_categories.forEach(function(course_category) {
      course_category.onclick = function(e) {
        var target_course_category = e.target.textContent.trim();
        isAreaElementClicked(target_course_category);
      }
    });
  }

  function isAreaElementClicked(target_course_category) {
      var impressions = [];

      if (datalayer_course_categories_context[target_course_category] !== undefined) {
          var relevant_courses = datalayer_course_categories_context[target_course_category];
          for (var i = 0; i < relevant_courses.length; i++) {
              var course_dict = relevant_courses[i];
              var course = convertDictToArray(course_dict)[0];
              impressions.push({
                  'id': course.code,
                  'name': course.name,
                  'category': course.category,
                  'position': course.position,
                  'brand': course.brand,
                  'price': course.price,
                  'list': course.list
              });
          }

          pushAreaInfoToDataLayer(impressions);
      }
      isCourseItemClicked();
  }

  function pushAreaInfoToDataLayer(impressions) {
    dataLayer.push({
      'event': 'productImpression',
      'ecommerce': {
        'currencyCode': 'AUD', 
        'impressions':  impressions,
      }
    });
  }

    var courses = [];
    var courses_dict = {};
    // Merging courses into one array
    convertDictToArray(datalayer_course_categories).forEach(function (category_courses) {
        courses = courses.concat(category_courses);
    });

    // Now merging all the data into a courses dictionary
    courses.forEach(function (course) {
        courses_dict = Object.assign({}, courses_dict, course);
    });

  function isCourseItemClicked() {
      var course_items = document.querySelectorAll(".second-submenu .mp-level a.course-title");

      course_items.forEach(function (course_item) {
          course_item.onclick = function (e) {
              e.stopPropagation();
              var target_course_item_name = e.target.innerHTML;
              var products = [];

              var course = courses_dict[target_course_item_name];

              products.push({
                  'id': course.code,
                  'name': course.name,
                  'category': course.category,
                  'position': course.position,
                  'brand': course.brand,
                  'price': course.price,
                  'list': course.list
              });

              pushCourseItemInfoToDataLayer(course.list, products);
          }
      });
  }

  function pushCourseItemInfoToDataLayer(list,products) {
    dataLayer.push({
      'event': 'productClick',
      'ecommerce': {
        'click': {
          'actionField': {'list': list},
          'products': products,
        }
      }
    });
  }

  function convertDictToArray(dict) {
      return Object.keys(dict).map(function (e) {
          return dict[e];
      });
  }
  
  $(window).load(function() {
    isCourseCategoryClicked();
  });
  </script>

			var arealkup = {}


			$('#form-1 [name=area]').change(function() {
				var form = $(this.form);


				form.find('[name=00NE0000000ma2v]').empty();
				if (form.find('[name=area]').val() == '') {
					form.find('[name=00NE0000000ma2v]').append('<option value="">\u002D\u002D Select Area \u002D\u002D</option>');
				} else {
					form.find('[name=00NE0000000ma2v]').append('<option value="">\u002D\u002D Select Course \u002D\u002D</option>');
					cs = lookup[form.find('[name=area]').val()]['courses'];
					for (c in cs) {
						if (!cs.hasOwnProperty(c)) continue;
						c = cs[c];
						var o = $('<option></option>');
						o.val(c[0]).text(c[1]);
						form.find('[name=00NE0000000ma2v]').append(o);
					}
					console.log(" +  I need help to decide + ");
					console.log(lookup[form.find('#id_area').val()]['code']);
					if(lookup[form.find('#id_area').val()]['code']) form.find('[name=00NE0000000ma2v]').append('<option value="' + lookup[form.find('#id_area').val()]['code'] + '">I need help to decide</option>');

					//form.find('[name=00NE0000000ma2v]').append('<option value="' + lookup[form.find('#id_area').val()]['code'] + '">I\'m not sure yet</option>');
					
				}
				try {
					form.find('[name=00NE0000000ma2v]').rules("add", {messages:{'required':'Please select a course'}});
				} catch (err) {
				}
			});
			$('#form-1').validate({focusInvalid:false, submitHandler:function(form){ dataLayer.push({'event': 'submitted'}); dataLayer.push({'StudyTimeframe': StudyTimeValue, 'event': 'rfitimeframeSelected'});dataLayer.push({'area_code': area_code, 'area_title': area_title, 'area_url': area_url, 'subarea_code': subarea_code, 'subarea_title': subarea_title, 'subarea_url': subarea_url, 'course_code': course_code,'course_title': course_title, 'course_url':course_url , 'event': 'leadselected'}); form.submit(); }});
			$('#form-1 input[name=first_name]').rules("add", {minlength: 2, not:'First Name', messages:{'required':'Please enter your first name', 'not':'Please enter your first name'}});
			$('#form-1 input[name=last_name]').rules("add", {minlength: 2, not:'Last Name', messages:{'required':'Please enter your last name', 'not':'Please enter your last name'}});
			$('#form-1 input[name=email]').rules("add", {messages:{'required':'Please enter an email', 'email':'Please enter a valid email'}});

       $(document).ready(function () {
        grecaptcha.ready(function () {
            var formId = '#form-2';
            $(formId).submit(recaptchaHandler);
            var submitEventList = $._data($(formId).get(0), "events").submit;

            //relocate this handler from tail to head of event list
            submitEventList.unshift(submitEventList.pop());

            function recaptchaHandler(event) {
                var form = event.target;
                if ($(form).valid()) {
                    event.stopImmediatePropagation();
                    event.preventDefault();
                    $(form).unbind("submit", recaptchaHandler);
                    grecaptcha.execute('6LeJ0KcZAAAAAOFnApoaSCiJIqdVCObLbiXrLubL', {action: 'homepageForm'}).then(function (token) {
                        $(formId + " #recaptcha").val(token);
                        $(form).triggerHandler('submit');
                        $(form).submit(recaptchaHandler);
                    });
                }
            }
        });
    });

        $("select#id_00NE0000000ma2v").change(function (e) {
            var selected_course = this.options[e.target.selectedIndex].text.trim();
            var form_id = this.closest('form').id;
            var form_element = $('#' + form_id);
            $(form_element).find("#id_trial_opt_in_check_box").prop("checked", false);
            $('.free-trial').addClass('hidden');
            sessionStorage.removeItem('trial_checkbox_value');

            if (courses[selected_course] && courses[selected_course]['available_for_trial'] === 'True') {
                $(form_element).find("#id_trial_opt_in_check_box").prop("checked", true);
                $('.free-trial').removeClass('hidden');
            }
        });

        
    });

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function getCookieValue(ckie, nme) {
					var splitValues;
					for (var i = 0; i < ckie.length; i++) {
						splitValues = ckie[i].split("=");
						var key = splitValues[0]
						key = key.replace(/^\s*/gi, "");
						if (key == nme) {
						  return splitValues[1];
						}
					}
					return 0;
				}
				function counterCookie() {
					  var adName = "rfiAdServeCountY";
					  var num_of_hours_to_save_cookie = 3;
					  var cookie = document.cookie;
					  var counter = 0;
					  var nvpair = cookie.split(";");
					  var checkCookie = parseInt(getCookieValue(nvpair,adName), 10);

					if (checkCookie != 0 || checkCookie != "") {
						counter = checkCookie;
					}

					  counter++;
					  var newCookieDate = new Date();
					  newCookieDate.setTime(newCookieDate.getTime()+(num_of_hours_to_save_cookie*60*60*1000));
					  var newCookie = adName + "=" + counter;
					  newCookie += "; expires=" + newCookieDate.toGMTString() + "; path=/";
					  window.document.cookie = newCookie;
					  return counter;
				}
  </script>
